             app.load('//newsletters.vocento.com/prospect/0700/js/prospect.js');
             app.when('consent:dmp').then(function(result) {
           if (result) {
             setTimeout(function() {app.load('//js.agkn.com/prod/v0/tag.js');}, 2000);
           }
         })
     });
   </script>
   <script>
    function setUpAgknTag(tag) {tag.setBpId("vocento");}
   </script>
